# *Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic*

[Edit](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic?veaction=edit) 

* [Edit source](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic?action=edit)
* [History](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic?action=history)
* [Purge](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic?action=purge)
* [Talk (288)](/wiki/Talk:Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic)

[![This article details a subject that falls under the Legends continuity.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "This article details a subject that falls under the Legends continuity.")[![The subject of this article takes place in the Old Republic era.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Old_Republic_era "The subject of this article takes place in the Old Republic era.")[![The subject of this article exists in or is relevant to the real world.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Category:Real-world_media "The subject of this article exists in or is relevant to the real world.")

This article is about **the [video game](/wiki/Star_Wars_video_games "Star Wars video games")**.  
You may be looking for **the various other [*Knights of the Old Republic*](/wiki/Knights_of_the_Old_Republic_(disambiguation) "Knights of the Old Republic (disambiguation)") projects**.

## Chronological information

### Timeline

### Next

*[Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic II: The Sith Lords](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic_II:_The_Sith_Lords "Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic II: The Sith Lords")*

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:VideoGame)

:   "*What greater weapon is there than to turn an enemy to your cause? To use their own knowledge against them?*"
:   ―[Bastila Shan](/wiki/Bastila_Shan "Bastila Shan") — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Greaterweapon2.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250308174658)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Greaterweapon2.flac "File:Greaterweapon2.flac"))[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

***Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic*** (***KotOR***) is a [roleplaying game](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_role-playing_game "wikipedia:Computer role-playing game") made originally for the [Microsoft](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft "wikipedia:Microsoft") [Xbox](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xbox "wikipedia:Xbox") and later released for the [PC](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Personal_computer "wikipedia:Personal computer") and [Mac OS X](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mac_OS_X "wikipedia:Mac OS X"), also available on [iOS](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iOS "wikipedia:iOS") and [Android](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Android_(operating_system) "wikipedia:Android (operating system)") devices. The game was developed by [BioWare](/wiki/BioWare "BioWare") and published by [LucasArts](/wiki/LucasArts "LucasArts") for Xbox on [July 15](/wiki/July_15 "July 15"), [2003](/wiki/2003 "2003"), for PCs running [Microsoft Windows](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft_Windows "wikipedia:Microsoft Windows") on [November 19](/wiki/November_19 "November 19"), 2003, and later for Mac OS X on [September 7](/wiki/September_7 "September 7"), [2004](/wiki/2004 "2004"). A decade later it was ported by [Aspyr Media](/wiki/Aspyr_Media "Aspyr Media"), first on iOS, in [May 30](/wiki/May_30 "May 30"), [2013](/wiki/2013 "2013"), and on Android in [December 23](/wiki/December_23 "December 23"), [2014](/wiki/2014 "2014"). Set [3,956 years before](/wiki/3956_BBY "3956 BBY") [*A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), *Knights of the Old Republic* covers the era just after that of the [*Tales of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(comic_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (comic series)") comics, the time of the ancient [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Galactic Republic/Legends").

*KotOR* is the first computer [RPG](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Role-playing_game "wikipedia:Role-playing game") set in the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* universe. It uses the [d20 System](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D20_System "wikipedia:D20 System"), from the [Wizards of the Coast](/wiki/Wizards_of_the_Coast "Wizards of the Coast") *[Star Wars Roleplaying Game](/wiki/Star_Wars_Roleplaying_Game "Star Wars Roleplaying Game")* rules. The game also allows the player to either be a servant to the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Light side of the Force/Legends") or the [dark side](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Dark side of the Force/Legends"), using an alignment system that tracks actions, from simple dialogue choices to major plot decisions. Combat is turn-based. Time is divided into discrete rounds, and combatants attack/react simultaneously. However, the number of actions a combatant may perform each round is limited. While the round's duration is a fixed short interval of real time (around six seconds), the player can configure the combat system to pause at specific events or at the end of each round.

A sequel - *[Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic II: The Sith Lords](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic_II:_The_Sith_Lords "Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic II: The Sith Lords")* - was developed by a different studio, [Obsidian Entertainment](/wiki/Obsidian_Entertainment "Obsidian Entertainment"), using an updated version of the Odyssey Engine from the first game. Bioware was occupied with producing [*Jade Empire*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jade_Empire "wikipedia:Jade Empire") and wanted to focus more on their original productions than licensed games, but they recommended Obsidian for *KotOR*'s sequel and retained limited oversight on Obsidian's development of *The Sith Lords*. It was released for Xbox a year later, in [December](/wiki/December "December") of 2004, and PC in [February](/wiki/February "February") of [2005](/wiki/2005 "2005"). On [September 9](/wiki/September_9 "September 9"), [2021](/wiki/2021 "2021"), Sony announced *[Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic – Remake](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic_%E2%80%93_Remake "Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic – Remake")*, a [PlayStation 5](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PlayStation_5 "wikipedia:PlayStation 5") remake of the original game developed by Aspyr Media.

## Opening crawl[]

| KNIGHTS OF THE OLD REPUBLIC |
| --- |
| ``` Four thousand years before the rise of the Galactic Empire, the Republic verges on collapse. DARTH MALAK, last surviving apprentice of the Dark Lord Revan, has unleashed an invincible Sith armada upon an unsuspecting galaxy.  Crushing all resistance, Malak's war of conquest has left the Jedi Order scattered and vulnerable as countless Knights fall in battle, and many more swear allegiance to the new Sith Master.  In the skies above the Outer Rim world of Taris, a Jedi battle fleet engages the forces of Darth Malak in a desperate effort to halt the Sith's galactic domination.... ``` |
|  |

## Plot summary[]

This is based on the [canonical](/wiki/Canon "Canon") [male](/wiki/Gender/Legends "Gender/Legends") [light side](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Light side of the Force/Legends") version of the game and assumes that the [planets](/wiki/Planet/Legends "Planet/Legends") are visited in the order [Dantooine](/wiki/Dantooine/Legends "Dantooine/Legends"), [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine/Legends "Tatooine/Legends"), [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk/Legends "Kashyyyk/Legends"), [Manaan](/wiki/Manaan/Legends "Manaan/Legends"), then [Korriban](/wiki/Korriban/Legends "Korriban/Legends"). Gender, order of planets visited and other variables can differ depending on the input of the player.

**This section of the article assumes that the player chooses only "[light side](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Light side of the Force/Legends")" options in the course of the game. Alternate stories are noted in the "[Behind the scenes](#Behind_the_scenes)" section. Note: The events in this section may or may not have been confirmed as [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") within the [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") continuity.**

### Trapped on Taris[]

:   ![Blue Glass Arrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D) *See also: [Attack on the Endar Spire](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Endar_Spire "Attack on the Endar Spire")*
:   ![Blue Glass Arrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D) *See also: [Rescue of Bastila Shan](/wiki/Rescue_of_Bastila_Shan "Rescue of Bastila Shan")*

 [![Carth Onasi](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Carth_Onasi_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20131201213015) [![Carth Onasi](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Carth_Onasi_profile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20131201213015)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Carth_Onasi_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20131201213015) 

Carth Onasi

 

A [soldier](/wiki/Revan/Legends "Revan/Legends") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Galactic Republic/Legends") wakes up to find himself in the middle of a [battle](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Endar_Spire "Attack on the Endar Spire") on the [*Hammerhead*-class capital ship](/wiki/Hammerhead-class_cruiser "Hammerhead-class cruiser") *[Endar Spire](/wiki/Endar_Spire "Endar Spire")*, which is on a mission under the [Jedi Sentinel](/wiki/Jedi_Sentinel/Legends "Jedi Sentinel/Legends") [Bastila Shan](/wiki/Bastila_Shan "Bastila Shan"). [Trask Ulgo](/wiki/Trask_Ulgo "Trask Ulgo"), another [Republic soldier](/wiki/Republic_soldier "Republic soldier"), aids his escape from the doomed vessel and splits off to face [Darth Malak](/wiki/Darth_Malak "Darth Malak")'s [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice/Legends "Sith apprentice/Legends") [Darth Bandon](/wiki/Darth_Bandon "Darth Bandon"). Trask seals the door behind him and buys his brother in arms time to escape. After entering the starboard section and finding [Carth Onasi](/wiki/Carth_Onasi "Carth Onasi") in the [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod/Legends "Escape pod/Legends") bay, the two join up and crash-land on the Sith-occupied [ecumenopolis](/wiki/Ecumenopolis/Legends "Ecumenopolis/Legends") of [Taris](/wiki/Taris/Legends "Taris/Legends"). Carth is able to drag the unconscious man from the wreckage and rent an abandoned apartment in the [Upper City](/wiki/Upper_City "Upper City"). The man remains in a stupor for the next few days.

 [![Bastila Shan](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/Bastila_Shan_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20140618180032) [![Bastila Shan](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/Bastila_Shan_profile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20140618180032)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/Bastila_Shan_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20140618180032) 

Bastila Shan

 

When the man regains consciousness, Carth informs him of the situation and that they need to find and [rescue Bastila](/wiki/Rescue_of_Bastila_Shan "Rescue of Bastila Shan"), whose escape pod has crash-landed somewhere on the planet. Bastila is and still would be, if rescued, the key to the Republic's war effort against the Sith due to her ability in [battle meditation](/wiki/Battle_meditation/Legends "Battle meditation/Legends"), a [Force power](/wiki/Force_power/Legends "Force power/Legends") that allows her to strengthen an entire army with confidence and spirit, while discouraging and confusing the enemy. Together, the two set out to find Bastila, and proceed into the hostile world.

The [soldier](/wiki/Soldier/Legends "Soldier/Legends") and Carth learn that Bastila's [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod") has landed in the [Undercity](/wiki/Undercity_(Taris) "Undercity (Taris)") of Taris—a rough area below the privileged [Upper City](/wiki/Upper_City "Upper City") and the slums of the [Lower City](/wiki/Lower_City "Lower City"), where two rival [swoop](/wiki/Swoop_racing/Legends "Swoop racing/Legends") gangs, the [Hidden Beks](/wiki/Hidden_Beks "Hidden Beks") and [Black Vulkars](/wiki/Black_Vulkars/Legends "Black Vulkars/Legends"), are engaged in a fierce [turf war](/wiki/Bek%E2%80%93Vulkar_gang_war "Bek–Vulkar gang war"). The fighting, plus the search for any other survivors of the battle, prompted the Sith to impose a security lockdown, forcing one of the pair to disguise himself in stolen [Sith trooper armor](/wiki/Sith_trooper_armor/Legends "Sith trooper armor/Legends") to gain entry to the area.

In the Lower City, the soldier and Carth go to the [Hidden Beks' hideout](/wiki/Hidden_Bek_Base "Hidden Bek Base"), where they find out from the leader of the Beks, [Gadon Thek](/wiki/Gadon_Thek "Gadon Thek"), that the Vulkar gang leader, [Brejik](/wiki/Brejik "Brejik"), has taken Bastila captive, intending to offer her as a prize for the winner of the [upcoming swoop race](/wiki/Tarisian_Season_Opener "Tarisian Season Opener"). Gadon agrees to sponsor the soldier as the Bek rider, on the condition that he retrieve a [prototype swoop-bike accelerator](/wiki/Prototype_accelerator "Prototype accelerator") that had been stolen from them by the Vulkars. In order to get to the back entrance of the [Black Vulkar Base](/wiki/Black_Vulkar_Base "Black Vulkar Base"), Gadon tells them to find the [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek/Legends "Twi'lek/Legends") girl [Mission Vao](/wiki/Mission_Vao "Mission Vao") and her [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee/Legends "Wookiee/Legends") friend [Zaalbar](/wiki/Zaalbar "Zaalbar"), who are supposed to know a way in through the Undercity of Taris, the lowest level of the city where criminals and refugees were exiled.

Coincidentally, when they find her, they discover that Mission needs their help as well. She and Zaalbar were attacked by [Gamorrean](/wiki/Gamorrean/Legends "Gamorrean/Legends") [slavers](/wiki/Slavery/Legends "Slavery/Legends") and Zaalbar had been captured as a result. Mission agrees to help them infiltrate the Vulkar Base if they help her find Zaalbar. The group ventures into the [sewers](/wiki/Undercity_sewers "Undercity sewers"). They track down and rescue Zaalbar from the slavers. Zaalbar, in gratitude, swears a Wookiee [life debt](/wiki/Life_debt/Legends "Life debt/Legends") to the soldier.

The group, led by Mission, heads deeper into the sewers to the back entrance of the Vulkar Base, which is guarded by a [rancor](/wiki/Rancor/Legends "Rancor/Legends"). They [raid the base](/wiki/Raid_on_the_Vulkar_Base "Raid on the Vulkar Base") and retrieve the accelerator after a confrontation with one of Brejik's lieutenants, [Kandon Ark](/wiki/Kandon_Ark "Kandon Ark"). Afterwards, they return to Gadon and the Beks, where they are offered to stay the night before going to the swoop track the next morning. The next day, the untested racer manages to win the race. Before he can accept his prize, however, Brejik forfeits the deal at the last moment, claiming the soldier had cheated by using the prototype accelerator. Amidst the chaos, Bastila breaks-free and a fight ensues; Brejik and his thugs cannot defeat them, and are slain in the skirmish.

Having rescued Bastila, the party begins looking for a way to get off Taris through the Sith blockade when a messenger comes to their apartment, telling them that a [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian/Legends "Mandalorian/Legends") [mercenary](/wiki/Mercenary/Legends "Mercenary/Legends"), [Canderous Ordo](/wiki/Canderous_Ordo "Canderous Ordo"), wants to speak with them in [Javyar's Cantina](/wiki/Javyar%27s_Cantina "Javyar's Cantina"). When they get there, Canderous proposes that they steal the *[Ebon Hawk](/wiki/Ebon_Hawk "Ebon Hawk")*, a freighter that belongs to his employer, [Davik Kang](/wiki/Davik_Kang "Davik Kang"), the Tarisian [Exchange](/wiki/Exchange "Exchange") boss. But first, they need the security pass codes to get through the Sith blockade, and the only place to get the codes is from the [Sith base](/wiki/Tarisian_military_base "Tarisian military base"). To gain entry into the base, they have to purchase [T3-M4](/wiki/T3-M4 "T3-M4"), a [T3-series utility droid](/wiki/T3-series_utility_droid "T3-series utility droid") that Davik has had programmed with the entrance codes to the base.

 [![Darth Malak](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Darth_Malak_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20131201213321) [![Darth Malak](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Darth_Malak_profile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20131201213321)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Darth_Malak_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20131201213321) 

Darth Malak

 

After purchasing T3-M4, the party breaks in and kills the [Sith Governor](/wiki/Sith_Governor "Sith Governor") to steal the passcodes. Canderous takes the soldier and Bastila to Davik's estate. Canderous recommends the soldier to Davik for hire as a ploy. Shortly after being welcomed, the three open the hangar doors and proceeded to steal the *Ebon Hawk*. Even as they do so, [Darth](/wiki/Darth/Legends "Darth/Legends") Malak, the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith/Legends "Dark Lord of the Sith/Legends"), now leading the Sith after betraying his former master Darth Revan, orders [Saul Karath](/wiki/Saul_Karath "Saul Karath"), [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral/Legends "Admiral/Legends") of the Sith Fleet, to [bombard](/wiki/Orbital_bombardment/Legends "Orbital bombardment/Legends")
Taris in order to prevent Bastila from escaping.

As they are getting to the *Ebon Hawk*, they are confronted by Kang and the [galaxy-wide](/wiki/The_galaxy/Legends "The galaxy/Legends") famous [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter/Legends "Bounty hunter/Legends") [Calo Nord](/wiki/Calo_Nord "Calo Nord") in the hangar. They kill Davik and leave Nord buried under rubble caused by the Sith bombardment. After stealing the *Ebon Hawk*, the infiltration party picks up the others and charges the Sith blockade while broadcasting the codes and escape the [Sith onslaught](/wiki/Destruction_of_Taris "Destruction of Taris").

### Dantooine refuge[]

Bastila reveals to the soldier that he is very strong in [the Force](/wiki/The_Force/Legends "The Force/Legends") and takes him back to the [Jedi Enclave](/wiki/Jedi_Enclave "Jedi Enclave") on Dantooine to see if the [Council](/wiki/Dantooine_Jedi_Enclave_Council "Dantooine Jedi Enclave Council") will train him as a [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi/Legends "Jedi/Legends"). They accept, in spite of his age, particularly after it is revealed that he is experiencing visions detailing the fall of Revan and Malak - and that he has shared these visions with Bastila, with whom he has forged a [Force bond](/wiki/Force-bond/Legends "Force-bond/Legends"). After training under [Zhar Lestin](/wiki/Zhar_Lestin "Zhar Lestin"), the soldier, now a Jedi-in-training, is charged with doing battle with [Juhani](/wiki/Juhani "Juhani"), a young Jedi apprentice who had been tainted by the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Dark side of the Force/Legends"). After defeating her, he succeeds in convincing her to return to the light and is promoted to the rank of [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan/Legends "Padawan/Legends").

He is then ordered by the Council to investigate [mysterious ruins](/wiki/Rakatan_ruins_(Dantooine) "Rakatan ruins (Dantooine)") that are believed to be the place seen in his visions. There, he finds a [droid](/wiki/Rakatan_guardian_droid "Rakatan guardian droid"), which requires him to pass two tests regarding his knowledge of astrography before proceeding further into the temple. The party completes these tasks successfully and is granted access into a room containing an incomplete [Star Map](/wiki/Star_Map "Star Map"). One which gives clues to the locations of four more, similar maps. The party surmises that the maps, if combined, would lead them to a mysterious "[Star Forge](/wiki/Star_Forge "Star Forge")" that the droid speaks of and which seems intricately tied to the fall of Revan and Malak. After learning of this, the Council charges the Padawan with the mission to find the Star Forge, accompanied by Bastila, his companions, and Juhani.

Meanwhile, unknown to them, Calo Nord, who has survived the carnage on Taris, is brought before Malak by Admiral Karath. Nord offers information to the Dark Lord about Bastila and her companions, which Saul promises Malak would find "most interesting." Malak agrees to hear this and to hire Nord to hunt down the party and bring Bastila to him alive.

### Second Star Map: Tatooine[]

The newly christened Padawan and his companions journey to the desert world, Tatooine, and explore the city of [Anchorhead](/wiki/Anchorhead/Legends "Anchorhead/Legends"). There, the Padawan receives another vision, indicating that the Star Map he is looking for is located in a cave. When learning that only hunters are allowed to leave the city, the Padawan persuades the head of the [Czerka](/wiki/Czerka_Arms/Legends "Czerka Arms/Legends") mining company there to hire him to eliminate the [Sand People](/wiki/Tusken_Raider/Legends "Tusken Raider/Legends") that have been plaguing the miners and other hunters in the area. However, a [Duros](/wiki/Duros/Legends "Duros/Legends") tells the Padawan that there might be a peaceful solution to the matter and urges him to find one.

 [![Anchorhead Settlement](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Anchorhead.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080910191333) [![Anchorhead Settlement](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Anchorhead.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080910191333)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Anchorhead.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080910191333) 

Anchorhead Settlement

 

Listening to the Duros' advice, the Padawan buys [HK-47](/wiki/HK-47 "HK-47"), an [HK-series assassin droid](/wiki/HK-series_assassin_droid "HK-series assassin droid"), thinly disguised as a [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid/Legends "Protocol droid/Legends") from the [town's droid shop](/wiki/Yuka_Laka%27s_Droid_Materials "Yuka Laka's Droid Materials") owner [Yuka Laka](/wiki/Yuka_Laka "Yuka Laka"). With the [droid's](/wiki/Droid/Legends "Droid/Legends") help, the player is able to communicate with a nearby tribe of Sand People at [their enclave](/wiki/Sand_People_Enclave "Sand People Enclave") and negotiates an end to the attacks on [Czerka Corporation](/wiki/Czerka_Arms/Legends "Czerka Arms/Legends") by giving the [Sand People chieftain](/wiki/Sand_People_chieftain "Sand People chieftain") two [moisture vaporators](/wiki/Moisture_vaporator/Legends "Moisture vaporator/Legends"). The chieftain then presents the party with his [Chieftain's gaderffii](/wiki/Chieftain%27s_gaderffii "Chieftain's gaderffii") as a sign of good faith, and a map that helps them locate a Star Map hidden in the [Eastern Dune Sea](/wiki/Eastern_Dune_Sea "Eastern Dune Sea"). The Padawan then follows this map to a [canyon krayt dragon's](/wiki/Canyon_krayt_dragon/Legends "Canyon krayt dragon/Legends") cave and assists a local hunter, [Komad Fortuna](/wiki/Komad_Fortuna "Komad Fortuna"), in killing it. He enters the [cave](/wiki/Rakatan_Ruins_(Tatooine) "Rakatan Ruins (Tatooine)") and acquires the second Star Map. As he and the others leave the cave they are confronted by Calo Nord and some other bounty hunters. Calo says he will have to kill them in spite of Malak's request that he take Bastila alive. The Padawan and his companions defend themselves, and kill Nord for good.

### Third Star Map: Kashyyyk[]

:   ![Blue Glass Arrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D) *See also: [Rebellion on Kashyyyk/Legends](/wiki/Rebellion_on_Kashyyyk/Legends "Rebellion on Kashyyyk/Legends")*

The Padawan then travels to Kashyyyk, and finds that the planet is under the control of Czerka Corporation, and that they are enslaving the local Wookiees. Hoping to enlist the aid of the Wookiees in reaching the [Shadowlands](/wiki/Shadowlands/Legends "Shadowlands/Legends") and the Star Map present there, the Padawan heads for the village of [Rwookrrorro](/wiki/Rwookrrorro/Legends "Rwookrrorro/Legends"). However, because he brings with him the accused [mad-claw](/wiki/Madclaw "Madclaw") Zaalbar into the city, he is seized and brought before the [Wookiee Chieftain](/wiki/Wookiee_Chieftain "Wookiee Chieftain"). The chieftain, [Chuundar](/wiki/Chuundar "Chuundar"), Zaalbar's brother, is secretly in league with Czerka. Chuundar blackmails the Padawan into hunting down a crazed Wookiee in the Shadowlands by keeping Zaalbar as a hostage. Fortunately for the Padawan, that gives him a chance to find the Star Map.

 [![Zaalbar](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Zaalbar_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20140618181537) [![Zaalbar](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Zaalbar_profile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/130?cb=20140618181537)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Zaalbar_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20140618181537) 

Zaalbar

 

In the Shadowlands, the Padawan meets an old hermit named [Jolee Bindo](/wiki/Jolee_Bindo "Jolee Bindo") who agrees to lead him to the Star Map in exchange for a favor: removing a group of Czerka poachers. The Padawan finishes the job and, as promised, Jolee lowers the [deflector shield](/wiki/Deflector_shield/Legends "Deflector shield/Legends") to let the party into the lower Shadowlands. When down there, the party discovers that the mad Wookiee is [Freyyr](/wiki/Freyyr "Freyyr"), Zaalbar and Chuundar's father who had exiled Zaalbar more than twenty years before as a mad-claw, only to discover the truth of Chuundar's treachery later. Having been driven from Rwookrrorro, Freyyr descended into the Shadowlands and when the party encounters him, he blindly attacks them and is defeated. However, the Padawan spares him and together they concoct a plan to get [Bacca's Ceremonial Blade](/wiki/Bacca%27s_Ceremonial_Blade "Bacca's Ceremonial Blade"), the symbol of a true chieftain, and fight Chuundar for the title. Freyyr says that the blade of the sword was lost in a ritual fight long ago against an [ancient beast](/wiki/Terentatek/Legends "Terentatek/Legends"). The party baits, finds the beast, and kills it. They then retrieve the blade from its hide. They give the blade to Freyyr, who then climbs up the trees towards Rwookrrorro, and asks the party to meet him there.

While in the Shadowlands, the Padawan discovers an ancient computer; whose [artificial intelligence](/wiki/Artificial_intelligence/Legends "Artificial intelligence/Legends") poses him a series of ethical dilemmas, whose "correct" answers reflect Sith philosophy. The Padawan's answers are deemed wrong by the computer, which sends out defense droids to terminate the intruder. However, when the party successfully defeats the ancient droids, the computer's scans of his brainwaves during the fight match those of the only person who is allowed to see the map. Thinking that the Padawan is that person, he allows the Padawan to see the Star Map.

Upon returning to the [lift](/wiki/Liftcar/Legends "Liftcar/Legends"), the party is forced to kill the Wookiee in charge of the basket, [Gorwooken](/wiki/Gorwooken "Gorwooken"), who has discovered their betrayal of Chuundar and attacks them. The party proceeds to the canopy on their own, meeting up with Freyyr's supporters on the way to Rwookrrorro. Upon arriving at the Chieftain's Hut, the room erupts in chaos, leading to a battle between the Padawan's allies and Czerka and Chuundar's loyalists, including himself. The Czerka and Wookiee bodyguards are slain along with Chuundar, and as a reward for their aid, Freyyr gives his only surviving son Bacca's Ceremonial Blade. Zaalbar is allowed to come out of exile and is no longer branded a madclaw. Shortly thereafter, the Wookiees of the village unite under their new chieftain, Freyyr, and [rebel against Czerka](/wiki/Rebellion_on_Kashyyyk/Legends "Rebellion on Kashyyyk/Legends") with the aid of the party.

Meanwhile, upon hearing the news of Calo Nord's death, Malak sends his apprentice, Darth Bandon, to take the bounty hunter's place as the leader in the search for Bastila.

### Fourth Star Map: Manaan[]

:   ![Blue Glass Arrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D) *See also: [Raid on the Sith Embassy](/wiki/Raid_on_the_Sith_Embassy "Raid on the Sith Embassy")*

Following their visit to Kashyyyk, the crew of the *Ebon Hawk* heads for the oceanic world of Manaan, landing in the [docking bay](/wiki/Manaan_Docking_Bay "Manaan Docking Bay"). The Padawan's visions indicated that the Star Map was on the ocean floor and hears the Republic ambassador to Manaan, [Roland Wann](/wiki/Roland_Wann "Roland Wann"), might have answers to his questions. Upon reaching the [embassy](/wiki/Republic_Embassy_(Manaan) "Republic Embassy (Manaan)") the party asks Roland about a means to reach it. Wann agrees to help them in exchange for retrieving a captured probe droid. The droid had been surfacing from a survey of the [Hrakert Rift](/wiki/Hrakert_Rift "Hrakert Rift"), a major source for Manaan's precious and unique resource, [kolto](/wiki/Kolto/Legends "Kolto/Legends"), and where the Star Map was, when it was captured by the Sith.

The Padawan agrees to help the Republic, [infiltrating](/wiki/Raid_on_the_Sith_Embassy "Raid on the Sith Embassy") the [Sith embassy](/wiki/Sith_Embassy "Sith Embassy") via one of three entrances, and fighting his way to the droid. The droid had been scavenged, but the part that Wann had requested is still intact. The party is leaving the base with droid part in hand when they are confronted by [Selkath](/wiki/Selkath/Legends "Selkath/Legends") authorities with reports of shots fired within the embassy. The Padawan is put on trial and despite being offered an arbiter to represent him, he single-handedly persuades the authorities to let him go. Now free, the Padawan proceeds back to the Republic embassy.

 [![A Selkath](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Selkath_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20130730150958) [![A Selkath](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Selkath_profile.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20130730150958)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Selkath_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20130730150958) 

A Selkath

 

The party learns from Roland that the droid was sent to investigate an illegal kolto harvesting plant that was created by the Republic and which had recently broken contact with the surface. He tells the Padawan that the Republic hired many mercenaries to investigate what happened at the station, but none had returned. He also informs the Padawan that they had lost contact with the facility after uncovering some ancient artifact. In exchange for help in investigating the facility, Roland provides the party with a [submersible](/wiki/Submarine/Legends "Submarine/Legends") and sends them on their way.

Once they arrive, the Padawan meets a crazed mercenary and learns from him that, following the artifact's excavation, the Selkath were going insane and killing everyone. Refusing to leave in spite of warnings, the Padawan fights his way through the facility and obtains an [enviro-suit](/wiki/Environment_suit/Legends "Environment suit/Legends") and a [sonic emitter](/wiki/Sonic_emitter/Legends "Sonic emitter/Legends") in the process. Forced to leave his companions behind, the Padawan searches the ocean floor with the one wet suit available and finds his way to a separate part of the facility.

There, he meets the head [scientist](/wiki/Scientist/Legends "Scientist/Legends"), [Kono Nolan](/wiki/Kono_Nolan "Kono Nolan") and his associate, [Sami](/wiki/Sami_(Human) "Sami (Human)"). The two are the only Human scientists still alive and are trapped in the facility. After surviving their mad attempt to kill him, the Padawan persuades them to tell him what they know. They inform him about a [massive firaxan shark](/wiki/Progenitor "Progenitor"), which is responsible for the Selkath's insanity. Upon asking how to get past it to the Star Map, Kono reveals that he had been working on a poison which, in theory, could kill the shark. Sami believes that using it would pollute the waters of Manaan in ways that may never be corrected. Following Sami's advice, the Padawan destroys the kolto harvesting machine, calming the shark down and allowing the Padawan to approach the Star Map.

When the Padawan is reunited with his companions at the entrance of the base, they meet Darth Bandon, accompanied by two [Dark Jedi](/wiki/Dark_Jedi/Legends "Dark Jedi/Legends"). After Bandon expresses his excitement that he could still "have the pleasure" of killing the Padawan, the party engages in a vicious [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel/Legends "Lightsaber duel/Legends") from which the Padawan emerges victorious. The Padawan returns to the Republic embassy and tells Roland of what had happened. Though displeased with the results, Roland thanks the Padawan and sends him on his way. The Padawan is again seized by the Selkath authorities, this time for his actions at the Kolto facility. Again, the Padawan persuades them to release him upon revealing the full story, which some of the Selkath believe tie into their myths surrounding "the Progenitor," which they believe the Padawan had saved.

### Revelation aboard the *Leviathan*[]

:   ![Blue Glass Arrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D) *See also: [Skirmish aboard the Leviathan](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Leviathan "Skirmish aboard the Leviathan")*

As the party leaves Manaan, they are caught in the tractor beam of the [*Leviathan*](/wiki/Leviathan_(Interdictor-class_cruiser) "Leviathan (Interdictor-class cruiser)"), the flagship of Admiral Saul Karath, Carth's old mentor. While they are being pulled in, they discuss how to escape and the Padawan picks a member of his party to escape the Sith and rescue everyone else from capture. The Padawan, Bastila, and Carth are all put in [force cages](/wiki/Force_cage "Force cage"), and are interrogated by Saul Karath himself as he waits for Malak's arrival. He also informs them that the [Jedi Academy on Dantooine has been destroyed](/wiki/Attack_on_Dantooine_(Jedi_Civil_War) "Attack on Dantooine (Jedi Civil War)"). Bastila refuses to submit to Karath's questions, so the Admiral questions the Padawan instead. For every question he answers incorrectly, Bastila is [tortured](/wiki/Torture/Legends "Torture/Legends"). The Padawan's will weakens, but ultimately the Sith receive little of use from the interrogation. Saul leaves and orders the trio's torture to be continued. The Padawan faints along with Bastila, and Carth informs him that he got the worst of the torture, and Bastila is worried that the dark side is growing stronger, because she did not sense a disturbance in the force when Dantooine was attacked. However, she senses that Saul sent his message to Darth Malak.

Meanwhile the party member is able to infiltrate the *Leviathan*, and get some weapons in the process. In the prison block, the party member finds a [Rodian](/wiki/Rodian/Legends "Rodian/Legends") who helps in the rescue in exchange for his freedom. He gives the party member the [ICE breaker](/wiki/ICE_breaker "ICE breaker"). The party member uses it to open the area that contains the Padawan and the others who, when freed, recover their equipment from lockers in the next room. Afterwards, Canderous volunteers to take the group to the *Ebon Hawk* and get it ready to launch, while the Padawan, Bastila, and Carth move to the bridge to disable the shields in the hangar bay.

After getting to the bridge by walking along the hull of the ship in environmental suits, the Padawan, Carth, and Bastila confront Admiral Karath and his men there. The Admiral confidently reveals that Malak's arrival is near and Bastila confirms it through the Force. An [urgent battle](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Leviathan "Skirmish aboard the Leviathan") follows, which the three manage to win. Saul, near death, asks his old student to come closer so he can reveal a secret. Curious, Carth leans in and with his dying breath Saul tells the soldier something that sends him into a fury. Carth confronts Bastila about what Saul had said, and Bastila begs Carth to wait until after they've escaped to talk about it, promising to explain everything. Reluctantly, Carth agrees, leaving the Padawan in the dark.

 [![The Ebon Hawk escapes from the Leviathan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Leviathan_Ebon_Hawk.png/revision/latest?cb=20130204121136) [![The Ebon Hawk escapes from the Leviathan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Leviathan_Ebon_Hawk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130204121136)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Leviathan_Ebon_Hawk.png/revision/latest?cb=20130204121136) 

The *Ebon Hawk* escapes from the *Leviathan*.

 

Before they are able to reach the hangar, they run into the Dark Lord, who disarms Carth in a standoff with Bastila and the Padawan. Then the Dark Lord says he is surprised to see the Padawan again, which confuses the Jedi-in-training. This amuses Malak who sneeringly reveals to the Padawan a truth that Bastila, the Jedi, and now Carth have been hiding from him: his true identity, the former Dark Lord of the Sith, Darth Revan. Malak, eager to kill his former Master once and for all, uses [Force Stasis Field](/wiki/Force_Stasis/Legends "Force Stasis/Legends") on Bastila and Carth, leaving Revan to fight the Dark Lord by himself. After a prolonged battle, Bastila releases herself and Carth. She charges in, telling Carth and Revan to escape so they can find the Star Forge. She then takes on the Dark Lord by herself and the door seals behind her, trapping her and stopping Revan and Carth from helping her.

Seeing nothing else that they can do, Revan and Carth run to the *Ebon Hawk*, and after a skirmish with [Sith fighters](/wiki/Sith_fighter "Sith fighter"), escape the *Leviathan*. Afterwards, the rest of the group learns the truth about their leader, meeting it with mixed but overall positive reactions. In a strange coincidence, HK-47's memory, which had been lost due to simulated damage to his [memory core](/wiki/Memory_bank/Legends "Memory bank/Legends"), was restored due to a program designed to do so upon returning to his first and true master: Revan.

### Fifth Star Map: Korriban[]

:   ![Blue Glass Arrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D) *See also: [Skirmish on Korriban](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Korriban "Skirmish on Korriban")*

Eager to acquire the last Star Map and find the Star Forge before it's too late, the group arrives on Korriban, a Sith world and the location of a [settlement](/wiki/Dreshdae "Dreshdae") and a [Sith Academy](/wiki/Sith_Academy_(Korriban) "Sith Academy (Korriban)"). Students from the Academy dominate the docking areas. These students, training to become Sith themselves, are encouraged to commit acts of cruelty and brutality. The most frequent victims of these acts are the new arrivals eager to join the Academy.

 [![.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/Dreshdae.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080527034824) [![.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/Dreshdae.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20080527034824)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/Dreshdae.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080527034824) 

[Dreshdae](/wiki/Dreshdae "Dreshdae").

 

Revan quickly surmises that the Star Map would be accessible only by a student of the Academy. Admittance requires gaining the notice of the student body and distinguishing oneself by means of strength, cunning, and/or ingenuity. Only one graduate is allowed to join the Academy each term so vicious and often fatal competition is encouraged by the [Sith Masters](/wiki/Sith_Master/Legends "Sith Master/Legends").

Revan finds help in this regard when he comes to the attention of [Yuthura Ban](/wiki/Yuthura_Ban "Yuthura Ban"), second-in-command at the Academy. She quickly notices the vast Force potential of her newest recruit although she does not realize that she is dealing with the deposed Dark Lord. She entangles Revan in a web of conspiracy whose ultimate goal is to engineer the assassination of [Uthar Wynn](/wiki/Uthar_Wynn "Uthar Wynn"), the head of the Sith Academy and Yuthura's master.

The potential students of the academy prove their worth by performing various tasks and gaining prestige. Some of the challenges are martial in nature while others were mental, but all require a certain commitment to the Sith ideals embodied by the [Code of the Sith](/wiki/Code_of_the_Sith/Legends "Code of the Sith/Legends") which Revan is required to relearn and recite in order to take an early lead over his fellow initiates. The Code of the Sith, a twist of the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code/Legends "Jedi Code/Legends"), is a harsh insight for Revan as much of its philosophy is based on ideals and motives he had set in motion as the Dark Lord.

At some point Revan, most likely in an attempt to receive prestige, explores and raids the [tomb](/wiki/Tomb_of_Ajunta_Pall "Tomb of Ajunta Pall") of the ancient [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord/Legends "Sith Lord/Legends") [Ajunta Pall](/wiki/Ajunta_Pall "Ajunta Pall"). This is complicated by the fact that the Sith Lord himself has survived the many centuries since his death as an embittered [Force ghost](/wiki/Force_ghost/Legends "Force ghost/Legends"). Ajunta Pall demands that Revan locate his [infamous blade](/wiki/Sword_of_Ajunta_Pall "Sword of Ajunta Pall"), taking it with him when he leaves the tomb. Revan retrieves the blade as well as two more besides. Revan then persuades the dark specter that he could at last find peace if he was willing to seek redemption. At last giving into the light, Ajunta fades away, redeemed by Revan.

Between Revan's actions and Yuthura's plotting, Revan eventually wins the prestige contest, gaining access to the tomb of [Naga Sadow](/wiki/Naga_Sadow/Legends "Naga Sadow/Legends") and the Star Map inside. There he finds the last of the Star Maps and finishes the last of the Academy's trials. Upon emerging he is forced to choose sides between Uthar and Yuthura and eventually defeats both of them, sparing Yuthura even after she betrays him following the death of Uthar Wynn. Upon leaving the tomb, all of the students of the academy [attack](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Korriban "Skirmish on Korriban") Revan; they are all slain. With his goals completed, Revan leaves the Sith world behind him, and sets a course for the Star Forge itself.

### Crash-landing on an unknown world[]

Armed with the location of the Star Forge, Revan and the crew of the *Ebon Hawk* arrive at the coordinates shown on the Star Maps, only to be trapped in a power disruption field that forces them to crash-land on [the planet that is the source of the disruption.](/wiki/Lehon/Legends "Lehon/Legends") Before they crash, Carth manages to send the coordinates of the Star Forge to the Republic so that they can gather a fleet to destroy the Sith forces located in the system.

 [![The Rakatan world at the time of Revan's second known landing.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/LehonBeach.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20050815145614) [![The Rakatan world at the time of Revan's second known landing.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/LehonBeach.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20050815145614)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/LehonBeach.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20050815145614) 

The Rakatan world at the time of Revan's second known landing.

 

They discover that the planet is a graveyard of crashed ships, many of which have been stripped and looted by other voyagers affected by the power disruption field. Damage to the *Ebon Hawk* requires Revan to find repair parts as well as the source of the disruptor field; not only does the field prevent the crew of the *Ebon Hawk* from escaping the planet, it also effectively cripples the Republic fleet on its way. Upon exploring the unknown world, Revan and his companions find that the world is inhabited by a species that call themselves the [Rakata](/wiki/Rakata/Legends "Rakata/Legends").

Revan discovers the Rakatans are divided into several tribes, one of which was [the Elders](/wiki/Elders_(Rakatan) "Elders (Rakatan)"), who maintain some of the technology from the Rakatan [Infinite Empire](/wiki/Infinite_Empire/Legends "Infinite Empire/Legends") that built the Star Forge. The Elders, few in number, are at war with another, more primitive tribe known as the [Black Rakata](/wiki/Black_Rakata "Black Rakata"). Revan discovers that during his previous visit to the world, he'd exploited both sides to gain access to the Star Forge and he struggles to regain the trust of the Elders. Upon helping them recover some of their number who have been kidnapped by [the One](/wiki/The_One "The One"), the leader of the Black Rakata, Revan convinces the Elders to aid him in entering the [Temple of the Ancients](/wiki/Temple_of_the_Ancients "Temple of the Ancients"), which is the source of the disruption field. Though he is required to enter alone, Juhani and Jolee, after receiving a vision that warned them that Revan was in danger, join him at the last minute against the Elders' protests. Together they enter the Temple.

Inside, the three find their way to the disruptor field controls, only to be confronted by Bastila who has fallen to the dark side. She has sworn herself to Darth Malak's service, Malak having used a combination of torture and preying on her arrogance, pride, and love for Revan to convince her that the Jedi are using and holding her back. In a tense confrontation, Revan is forced to defend the light from the very person most responsible for his redemption. He reluctantly engages her in a duel, but with Juhani and Jolee's help, he defeats Bastila, who expresses surprise at Revan's power and comes to believe that he deserves to be the Dark Lord of the [Sith](/wiki/Darth_Revan%27s_Sith_Empire "Darth Revan's Sith Empire"). Bastila tries to seduce him back to the dark side, even going so far as to pledge her loyalty to him and promising him that she would use her Battle meditation in his service and become his apprentice and lover. Despite her temptations, Revan rejects her offer, and Bastila angrilly flees in a [G-wing](/wiki/G-Type_light_shuttle "G-Type light shuttle"), swearing that their next encounter aboard the Star Forge will be their last.

Escaping the temple and rejoining his companions, Revan and the others join the Republic's [assault on the Star Forge](/wiki/Battle_of_Rakata_Prime "Battle of Rakata Prime") knowing that the fate of the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy/Legends "Galaxy/Legends") rested on their efforts. However, for Revan, the battle was a personal conflict since saving the galaxy might mean taking the life of the woman he loved.

### The Star Forge[]

:   ![Blue Glass Arrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D) *See also: [Battle of Rakata Prime](/wiki/Battle_of_Rakata_Prime "Battle of Rakata Prime")*

 [![The Star Forge](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Sf-battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080203073214) [![The Star Forge](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Sf-battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20080203073214)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Sf-battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080203073214) 

The Star Forge

 

Admiral [Forn Dodonna](/wiki/Forn_Dodonna "Forn Dodonna") and [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master/Legends "Jedi Master/Legends") [Vandar](/wiki/Vandar_Tokare "Vandar Tokare") are mystified by the sheer size and efficiency of the [Sith fleet](/wiki/Sith_armada_(Jedi_Civil_War) "Sith armada (Jedi Civil War)") and, upon regaining contact with the *Hawk* and her crew, are horrified to learn of Bastila's defection. To counter the threat presented by Bastila, the Republic commanders come up with a desperate plan. The *Ebon Hawk* will lead a strike force of Jedi through the static defenses of the Star Forge. Only a handful of ships actually survive the run to land safely on the Star Forge's flight deck where Dark Jedi backed up by the station's battle droids attack the Jedi in the hangar. The Dark Jedi are defeated and the Jedi strike team is assigned to defend the hangar so they can later make their escape. Revan and two of his companions advance into the Star Forge and find themselves alone against the bulk of Darth Malak's entire fighting force, they battle wave after wave as they make their way towards Bastila.

Finally, Revan and the others reach Bastila's chamber where he is separated from his companions and left to confront Bastila alone. Bastila draws on all of her skills and the dark power of the Star Forge, but is ultimately unable to defeat Revan. Through their love for one another and the bond between them, Revan is able to break Bastila's resolve and persuades her to turn back to the light. In return, Bastila admits her love for Revan as well and promises to use her Battle meditation to aid the Republic fleet. Revan then leaves to confront his old friend and apprentice—Malak.

Malak tries once more to delay Revan by unleashing more battle droids upon him, but Revan proves more resilient than he had expected, making it past them and into Malak's chamber. A long duel ensues. Revan starts to overpower Malak who uses the technology of the Star Forge and the bodies of Jedi he had captured from the Jedi academy on Dantooine to fuel his power, restoring his lifeforce and strength to maximum levels. Revan releases the suffering Jedi one by one by destroying the machines containing them and allows them to become one with the Force. Malak is forced to rely on his own dark power and after a long battle, Revan finally succeeds in defeating Malak who expresses regret in his last moments before dying.

Afterwards, Revan flees along with the rest of his companions, barely escaping the final destruction of the Star Forge. The entire group is awarded the [Cross of Glory](/wiki/Cross_of_Glory "Cross of Glory"), the highest citation of bravery in the galaxy at the time, in a ceremony on the unknown world's surface and Revan himself is welcomed back into the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order/Legends "Jedi Order/Legends") as the "Prodigal Knight."

Assumption ends here.

## Major characters ‡[]

This is based on the canonical male light side version of the game.

**This section of the article assumes that the player chooses only "[light side](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Light side of the Force/Legends")" options in the course of the game. Alternate stories are noted in the "[Behind the scenes](#Behind_the_scenes)" section. Note: The events in this section may or may not have been confirmed as [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") within the [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") continuity.**

### Revan[]

:   "*The Dark Lord Revan is dead. I am a servant of the light now.*"
:   ―Revan[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Revan](/wiki/Revan/Legends "Revan/Legends")
[![Revanmemory](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/Revanmemory.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081030190414)

**Revan** is the main protagonist of *Knights of the Old Republic*. As the Dark Lord of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith/Legends "Sith/Legends") and Master of Darth Malak, Revan was led into a trap where a [Jedi strike team](/wiki/Jedi_strike_team_(Capture_of_Darth_Revan) "Jedi strike team (Capture of Darth Revan)"), led by [Bastila Shan](/wiki/Bastila_Shan "Bastila Shan"), infiltrated his [flagship](/wiki/Darth_Revan%27s_flagship "Darth Revan's flagship") and, unknowingly helped by Revan's own apprentice, [captured](/wiki/Capture_of_Darth_Revan "Capture of Darth Revan") him. Revan was badly wounded and his mind was [nearly destroyed](/wiki/Amnesia/Legends "Amnesia/Legends") from the battle, so the [Jedi Council](/wiki/Jedi_Council/Legends "Jedi Council/Legends"), in a bold move, programmed him with a new identity, one that is loyal to the Galactic Republic. Enlisted as a Republic soldier, Revan is caught up in events that lead him to rejoin the Jedi Order as a Padawan and travel the galaxy in search of enigmatic Star Maps in an attempt to foil the efforts of the Sith Empire. During his journey he is accompanied by various beings who are all determined to help him in his quest, especially Bastila Shan, with whom he developed a Force bond. Along the way, Revan is continuously confronted with situations that test his loyalty to the Jedi Order and the light side of the Force. Inevitably, the amnesiac Revan's memories begin to surface and he unearths his past, hidden from him by the combined efforts of the Jedi Order's lead Masters. The quest reaches a climax atop the Temple of the Ancients on the planet of Lehon, where Revan ultimately rejects the Dark side of the Force and travels to the Star Forge, a large [space](/wiki/Realspace/Legends "Realspace/Legends") factory that the Sith Empire is using to construct a conquest fleet, and confronts his former apprentice, Malak. Revan and his companions prove to be victorious and Revan is proclaimed the **Prodigal Knight** by the Jedi. For his efforts in destroying the Star Forge he is awarded the Republic's highest honor, the Cross of Glory.

### Darth Malak[]

:   "*Wipe this pathetic planet from the face of the galaxy.*"
:   ―Darth Malak ordering the destruction of [Taris](/wiki/Taris/Legends "Taris/Legends")[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Darth Malak](/wiki/Darth_Malak "Darth Malak")
[![DarthMalakartwork](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/DarthMalakartwork.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120205231239)

**Darth Malak** is introduced as the reigning Dark Lord of [his time](/wiki/Jedi_Civil_War "Jedi Civil War") and is the main antagonist. After following his former Sith Master, Revan, throughout the [Mandalorian Wars](/wiki/Mandalorian_Wars "Mandalorian Wars") and even to the dark side of the Force, this former [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight/Legends "Jedi Knight/Legends"), believing himself to be stronger and more deserving, usurps Revan's title of Dark Lord, by ordering his own ships to fire upon the Dark Lord while the latter defends himself against the Jedi strike team led by Bastila Shan. Malak felt confident that he would destroy both of his enemies at the same time. With his new position among the Sith, Darth Malak ruthlessly and systematically begins his reign of terror, either subduing or destroying the planets of the galaxy, his forces apparently limitless. Eventually, he learns that Bastila had not died in the attack, and desiring her Battle Meditation, begins a galaxy-wide hunt for her. Time and time again she eludes his capture and Malak becomes intrigued by the rumors of her new companions. Malak charges his Admiral, Saul Karath, with the task of capturing the group, which he does in an ambush from the bridge of Malak's flagship, the *Leviathan*. Here it is revealed that the now redeemed Revan, in fact, did not die in the attack. In a series of events, Malak is finally able to capture Bastila and turn her to the dark side under continued torture. Retreating to the Star Forge with his new apprentice, Malak fully intends to end the life of his former master and destroy the Republic with Bastila's Battle Meditation. His plans are shattered when Revan is able to bring Bastila back to the light side and he forfeits his life in a final battle with his former master, Revan.

### Saul Karath[]

:   "*In war even the innocent must die.*"
:   ―Saul Karath[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Saul Karath](/wiki/Saul_Karath "Saul Karath")
[![SaulKarathPro](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/SaulKarathPro.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081011044027)

**Saul Karath** was a famous Republic Admiral, mentor to Carth Onasi, who became a turncoat after he [bombarded Telos IV](/wiki/Bombing_of_Telos_IV "Bombing of Telos IV") as a show of faith for his new allies, the Sith. This led Carth down a dark path as it killed his [wife](/wiki/Morgana_Onasi "Morgana Onasi") and caused his [son](/wiki/Dustil_Onasi "Dustil Onasi") to go missing. Karath replaced [another Admiral](/wiki/Saul_Karath%27s_predecessor "Saul Karath's predecessor") as leader of the Sith Fleet, reporting directly to Darth Malak. On Malak's orders, he coordinated the destruction of Taris. He hired Calo Nord to hunt down the amnesiac Revan. When Calo failed to do this, Saul submitted himself to Malak and was spared. Later, after Revan found the third Star Map, the *Ebon Hawk* was pulled into Karath's flagship, the *Leviathan*, via [tractor beam](/wiki/Tractor_beam/Legends "Tractor beam/Legends"). The crew was captured, save one unknown by Karath, and Saul personally interrogated Bastila, Carth, and Revan. He used Revan's love for Bastila as a weakness, torturing Bastila every time Revan answered his questions incorrectly. He stopped the interrogation but continued the torture, waiting for the arrival of Darth Malak. The trio escaped with the assistance of the other party member and fought their way to the bridge. Karath, after informing them that Malak would be there momentarily, engaged the three and was beaten. Moments from death, he called Carth over and revealed a secret to him. His trusted leader, the first person Carth had opened up to in years, was Darth Revan.

### Bastila Shan[]

:   "*I'm Bastila Shan, a member of the Jedi Order and a fleet commander for the Republic. Nobody 'owns' me!*"
:   ―Bastila Shan[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Bastila Shan](/wiki/Bastila_Shan "Bastila Shan")
[![Bastila](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Bastila.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090503150002)

**Bastila Shan** is a young Jedi Knight proficient from a young age in battle meditation who enters the story after she is saved by Revan from the Black Vulkars on Taris. She leads Revan to the Jedi Academy on Dantooine and encourages the council to take him on as a [Jedi Initiate](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate/Legends "Jedi Initiate/Legends"), which they reluctantly agree to do. Bastila and Revan realize that they share a Force bond that allows them to share visions of the Star Maps. Over the course of the party's adventure, she shows signs of rashness and vanity, as well as an attraction to Revan that culminates in a kiss aboard the *Ebon Hawk*. She is captured aboard the *Leviathan* after it is revealed that she preserved Revan's life after Malak betrayed Revan. She is tortured for several days by Darth Malak himself in an attempt to turn her to the dark side. He is successful, as Revan finds out atop the Temple of the Ancients when she tries in vain to convince him to join her. He refuses, and she flees from him to the Star Forge. Inside the space station, she uses her battle meditation to assist the Sith fleet while rendering the Republic forces less effective. Revan fights his way to her and they engage in a long duel. Revan overpowers her several times and uses their bond and love for one another to turn her away from the dark side. She then uses her battle meditation against the Sith fleet and is awarded the Cross of Glory in the end for assisting the [Republic Fleet](/wiki/Republic_Navy/Legends "Republic Navy/Legends").

### Carth Onasi[]

:   "*I'm not a warrior, I'm a soldier. There's a difference. Warriors attack and conquer, they prey on the weak. Soldiers defend and protect the innocent—usually from warriors.*"
:   ―Carth to [Canderous Ordo](/wiki/Canderous_Ordo "Canderous Ordo")[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Carth Onasi](/wiki/Carth_Onasi "Carth Onasi")
[![Carth Taris](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/Carth_Taris.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081010161247)

**Carth Onasi** is an intensely loyal [Commander](/wiki/Commander/Legends "Commander/Legends") and expert [pilot](/wiki/Pilot/Legends "Pilot/Legends") with the Republic at the time of his escape in an escape pod with one other soldier, the mind-wiped Revan, to [Taris](/wiki/Taris/Legends "Taris/Legends") after the attack on the Endar Spire. Thus begins Carth's involvement in the adventure that will ultimately become a quest for the Star Maps and the destruction of the Star Forge. After escaping the attack on Taris aboard a stolen starship, the *Ebon Hawk*, Carth, Revan, Bastila and an ever growing number of companions, make their way to Dantooine, where Revan begins his training as a Jedi and Carth is officially assigned as pilot to the *Ebon Hawk*. Throughout the journey, Carth slowly reveals to Revan his past and obsession with killing his former mentor, Saul Karath, who is one of the individuals he blames for the death of his wife during the bombing of Telos IV. He comes to view Revan as a friend and is devastated when the group is captured aboard the *Leviathan* and Saul reveals to him that Revan is in fact the former Dark Lord of the Sith, before exacting his revenge on Saul. Carth is forced to reexamine his views regarding himself and Revan and comes to the conclusion that neither one of them are the same man they used to be and vows to help save Revan from himself and destroy the Star Forge. After the Battle of Rakata Prime, Carth is awarded the Cross of Glory and is promoted to Admiral.

### Canderous Ordo[]

:   "*I've killed many people. I can't say I'm proud of it, but I have. Criminals, competitors, businessmen, police… women, children…*"
:   ―Canderous Ordo[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Canderous Ordo](/wiki/Canderous_Ordo "Canderous Ordo")
[![Canderoustattoo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/Canderoustattoo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081011034249)

**Canderous Ordo** is a jaded Mandalorian war veteran working as a mercenary for Exchange [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord/Legends "Crime lord/Legends") Davik Kang on Taris. He finds no honor nor challenge in his work and as the [Sith occupy Taris](/wiki/Capture_of_Taris "Capture of Taris"), Canderous is more than ready to leave. He forms an ingenious plan to steal Davik's flagship, the *Ebon Hawk* and approaches Revan for help, claiming that only Revan has the necessary skills to follow the plan through to completion. Canderous travels with the group to Dantooine and decides that he will continue traveling with the Jedi, his former enemy, claiming that he will finally find worthy adversaries. His blunt personality and firm belief in the [Mandalorian code](/wiki/Mandalorian_Crusaders#Doctrine_and_organization "Mandalorian Crusaders") causes friction between him and the rest of the crew, most notably Carth Onasi and Bastila Shan. In searching for the Star Maps, Canderous's respect for Revan grows and he gradually reveals details of his life to him. On the planet of Tatooine, Canderous's integrity is challenged by [Jagi](/wiki/Jagi "Jagi"), a former subordinate from the Mandalorian War and he is called out to a duel. Revan's intervention is the deciding factor in the duel, for which he is grateful, yet compels him to rethink his Mandalorian beliefs. The revelation of Revan's past, after their escape from the *Leviathan* only serves to further cement Canderous's loyalty to Revan. He doesn't bother with distinctions between *light* and *dark*. To Canderous, there is only conviction that there is nothing more honorable than to fight for whom he considers to be the greatest warrior of their time. His involvement during the battle to destroy the Star Forge earns him the Cross of Glory.

### Mission Vao[]

:   "*Hey, don't treat me like I'm a little girl. I ain't no kid—I'm fourteen years old.*"
:   ―Mission Vao[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Mission Vao](/wiki/Mission_Vao "Mission Vao")
[![Mission Vao profile](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/Mission_Vao_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20131201210408)

**Mission Vao** is a young, wise-cracking, Twi'lek street urchin from the Lower City of Taris, who had been brought there as a very young child, and later abandoned by her shifty older brother [Griff](/wiki/Griff_Vao "Griff Vao"). She is originally recruited by Revan to use her less-than-reputable skills to gain entrance to the Black Vulkar base as part of a plan to rescue Bastila, but quickly becomes a permanent companion after her best friend, the Wookiee Zaalbar, pledges a life debt to Revan. She escapes the destruction of Taris and travels to Dantooine along with the other companions aboard the *Ebon Hawk*. At the Jedi Enclave she is recognized by her brother's former girlfriend, [Lena](/wiki/Lena "Lena"), and learns that her brother was last seen on Tatooine. She tells Revan that she would very much like to find her brother and Revan agrees, finding it difficult to deny the cheerful girl. Despite her difficult childhood filled with lies and betrayals, Mission is bubbly and optimistic, often seeing the good in people, especially while tracking down her ne'er-do-well brother. Her independent and sometimes mischievous nature at times created some friction with Carth and Bastila, but they both cared for her and acknowledged the usefulness of her skills. Mission is one of the companions that is least disturbed by the revelation of Revan's past, claiming that he isn't the Dark Lord anymore, and she would stick by him for everything that he had done for her. For her part in the Battle of Rakata Prime, Mission is also awarded the Cross of Glory.

### Zaalbar[]

:   «*Unless you want someone threatened or a door bashed in, you should ask someone else.*»
:   ―Zaalbar to Revan, on his abilities.[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Zaalbar](/wiki/Zaalbar "Zaalbar")
[![Zaalbar on Lehon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Zaalbar_on_Lehon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081010230907)

**Zaalbar** is the son of Wookiee Chieftain Freyyr and was born on the planet of Kashyyyk. He had been banished from his clan and labeled a madclaw for dishonorably using his claws to attack, before coming to Taris. He met Mission when she berated Black Vulkar gang members who were harassing him in the Lower City of Taris and the two became inseparable, with Zaalbar taking on the role of the young Twi'lek's protector. Shortly before the orbital bombardment of Taris, he is captured by Gamorrean slavers in the Undercity sewers. He is rescued by Revan, who had been persuaded to help by Mission. After overcoming his initial surprise at meeting another individual who speaks [Shyriiwook](/wiki/Shyriiwook/Legends "Shyriiwook/Legends"), Zaalbar promptly pledges a life debt to Revan. The search for the Star Maps takes the companions to his homeworld of Kashyyyk, where Revan aids the Wookiees in expelling Czerka slavers and the restoration of Freyyr as Chieftain. Zaalbar is once again accepted by his clan and is looked upon as the successor of Freyyr. Despite this, he once again reaffirms his life debt to Revan, vowing to return to Kashyyyk only after the destruction of the Star Forge, for which he is granted the Cross of Glory.

### Jolee Bindo[]

:   "*I'm old, dammit. I'm allowed to be enigmatic when I want to be!*"
:   ―Jolee Bindo[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Jolee Bindo](/wiki/Jolee_Bindo "Jolee Bindo")
[![JoleeHalfBody](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/JoleeHalfBody.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20071217235022)

**Jolee Bindo** is an aging Jedi who has spent the last twenty years in a self-imposed exile deep in the Shadowlands of Kashyyyk. Revan first encounters Jolee during his search for the Star Map on Kashyyyk, during which Jolee's help is necessary. Cryptic and close-mouthed about his past, other than revealing that he had fought the Sith in the [Great Sith War](/wiki/Great_Sith_War/Legends "Great Sith War/Legends"), Jolee announces his intention to travel with Revan claiming that he can see the swirl of destiny surrounding the Padawan and is curious to discover how it will end. Throughout the adventure, Jolee gradually reveals pieces of his past. He tells Revan of his days as a smuggler and his reasons for leaving the Jedi Order, effectively labeling him as a [Gray Jedi](/wiki/Gray_Jedi "Gray Jedi"). His most startling revelation concerns his wife, [Nayama](/wiki/Nayama "Nayama") and her fall to the dark side. Jolee is adamant in his conviction that love is important and advises Revan to remember that. The revelation of Revan's past is no surprise to him, since he had already come to that conclusion earlier. He believes that the Force wants him to help Revan and that impression is reinforced at the Temple of the Ancients, at which he experiences a [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision/Legends "Force vision/Legends") that prompts him and Juhani to accompany Revan into the temple. His participation in the destruction of the Star Forge earns him the Cross of Glory.

### Juhani[]

:   "*We WILL defeat Malak and save the Republic from the Sith threat once and for all!*"
:   ―Juhani on the [Temple of the Ancients](/wiki/Temple_of_the_Ancients "Temple of the Ancients")[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Juhani](/wiki/Juhani "Juhani")
[![Juhani crop](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/Juhani_crop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080304045344)

**Juhani** is a volatile [Cathar](/wiki/Cathar/Legends "Cathar/Legends") Jedi Knight who joins Revan and his companions in their quest to find the Star Maps after she is pulled back from the dark side during the amnesiac Revan's final test to become a Padawan on Dantooine. As an infant, Juhani's parents had fled with her from their homeworld of [Cathar](/wiki/Cathar_(location)/Legends "Cathar (location)/Legends"), after the [Battle of Cathar](/wiki/Battle_of_Cathar "Battle of Cathar") during the Mandalorian Wars, to Taris. The death of her father forces her mother into taking loans from the Exchange and when her mother dies, Juhani is sold into slavery to pay off the debts. She is rescued from this fate by the Jedi who come to Taris during the [Liberation of Taris](/wiki/Liberation_of_Taris "Liberation of Taris"). Enamored by the charismatic leader of the Jedi, who she later finds out was Revan, Juhani vows to become one herself and makes her way to the Jedi Enclave at Dantooine. She is eventually taken on as a Padawan by Jedi Master [Quatra](/wiki/Quatra "Quatra"), who recognizing the difficulty a Cathar has in reconciling their hot-tempered nature with the Jedi code, allows Juhani to believe she had been killed by her in an aggressive duel. Distraught by her actions, Juhani falls to the dark side until her fateful meeting with Revan. After her redemption, Juhani learns that her master had not been killed and it was but a final test. She realizes that she must let go of her anger and finally does so with Revan's help after sparing the life of the individual, [Xor](/wiki/Xor "Xor"), who was responsible for her father's death and was to buy her as a slave. The revelation of Revan's past only serves to strengthen Juhani's resolve to not give into the dark side and she, along with [Jolee](/wiki/Jolee "Jolee"), plays an important role in aiding Revan at the Temple of the Ancients on Lehon. Juhani is awarded the Cross of Glory for her role in the destruction of the Star Forge.

### HK-47[]

:   "*Disclosure: I am a versatile protocol and combat droid, fluent in verbal and cultural translation. Should your needs prove more... practical, I am also skilled in highly personal combat.*"
:   ―HK-47 sells himself[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [HK-47](/wiki/HK-47 "HK-47")
[![HK-47 profile](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/HK-47_profile.png/revision/latest?cb=20131201214732)

**HK-47** is a Hunter-Killer [assassin droid](/wiki/Assassin_droid/Legends "Assassin droid/Legends") that is built by Revan towards the end of the Mandalorian Wars and is used not only to dispatch his enemies, but also as a [Jedi hunter](/wiki/Jedi_hunter/Legends "Jedi hunter/Legends") during the Jedi Civil War. Sometime before Revan's capture by the Jedi, HK-47 is sent on an unknown assassination assignment and is lost. He eventually finds himself in the shop of Yuka Laka, an Ithorian who fitted HK with a [restraining bolt](/wiki/Restraining_bolt/Legends "Restraining bolt/Legends"). He sat in the shop's corner for a while swearing revenge against Yuka for the bolt and unwittingly claiming to have been built by [Systech Corporation](/wiki/Systech_Corporation/Legends "Systech Corporation/Legends") until an amnesiac Revan walked in the door during his search for the Star Forge. Revan purchased HK from Yuka and noticed problems with his memory core, it was missing data. HK is bought by Revan for his knowledge of the Sand People dialect and is instrumental in brokering an end to the Sand People attacks on Anchorhead. Revan is eventually able to restore some of his skills and lost experiences. It turned out that HK had been in the service of many important people such as a [senator](/wiki/Unidentified_Human_senator "Unidentified Human senator"), a [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt/Legends "Hutt/Legends") named [Bochaba](/wiki/Bochaba "Bochaba"), and a [low level Systech officer](/wiki/Unidentified_Systech_Corporation_officer "Unidentified Systech Corporation officer"), they also learned that HK had personally killed most of his former masters. After a certain point, Revan can no longer repair him and he stays a member of the party through the events aboard the Leviathan. After the amnesiac Revan learns of his former identity, more of HK's memory returned as it was programmed to do after he again knowingly meets his former master and true creator. The revelation that Revan is in fact his original master is the stimulus needed to fully unlock his memory. He is pleased to be reunited with his master and accompanies Revan for the rest of the journey.

### T3-M4[]

:   "*Dwoooo....*"
:   ―[T3-M4](/wiki/T3-M4 "T3-M4")[[10]](#cite_note-KOTOR-10)

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [T3-M4](/wiki/T3-M4 "T3-M4")
[![T3M4portrait](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/T3M4portrait.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070325052159)

**T3-M4** is a T3-series [utility droid](/wiki/Cleaning_droid/Legends "Cleaning droid/Legends") who is built and customized by [Janice Nall](/wiki/Janice_Nall "Janice Nall") on Taris to be a master [slicer](/wiki/Slicer/Legends "Slicer/Legends").
